Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 19, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











There is more to this event than just the [Top 8](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpshi17/top-8-decklists-2017-03-19). Below are the decklists of the players who finished in 9th through 32nd place. All of the Top 16 players had 39 points, so they all earned an invitation and airfare to Pro Tour *Hour of Devastation* in July. All of the Top 32 players had 37 or 36 points.







#### Kobayashi, Tomoya (Mardu Tokens)


##### 
 Grand Prix Shizuoka 2017 Spring 9th Place






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)





[Decklist](#none)
[Stats](#none)
[Sample Hand](#none)
